        function applyRefreshedSlotsToConfig(prebidAdUnit, gptSlots) {
            for (var slotIndex in gptSlots) {
                if (gptSlots[slotIndex].isRefreshed) {
                    for (var index in prebidAdUnit) {
                        if (prebidAdUnit[index].code === gptSlots[slotIndex].divId) {
                            var slotDefinitions = JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(prebidAdUnit[index]));
                            slotDefinitions.code = gptSlots[slotIndex].secondDivId;
                            prebidAdUnit.push(slotDefinitions);
                            break;
                        }
                    }
                }
            }

            return prebidAdUnit;
        }

        var getBid = function(bid, floor) {
            if (bid <= floor) {
                return 0;
            }
            return bid;
        };

        var bidConfig = {};
        for (var code in bidData) {
            bidConfig[code] = {
                bidCpmAdjustment : (function (bidRate, bidFloor) {
                    return function (bidCpm, bidObj) {
                        var bid = bidCpm * bidRate;
                        for (var slotId in bidFloor) {
                            if (slotId === bidObj.adUnitCode) {
                                return getBid(bid, bidFloor[slotId]);
                            }
                        }
                        return 0;
                    }
                }(bidData[code].bidRate, bidData[code].bidFloor))
            }
        }

                        if (refreshViewabilitySlot === undefined) {
                            var refreshViewabilitySlot = function (slotId, slot, element) {
                                var rect = element.getBoundingClientRect();
                                var sizes = JSON.parse(slot.adUnitSizes);
                                var height = sizes[0][1] * 0.2;
                                var position = rect.top - window.innerHeight + height;

                                var isOfferedOnPrebidAuctions = function (id) {
                                    for (var index in window.adUnits) {
                                        if (window.adUnits[index].code === id) {
                                            return true;
                                        }
                                    }
                                    return false;
                                };

                                if (position <= 0 && rect.top - height > 0) {
                                    googletag.cmd.push(function () {
                                        googletag.destroySlots([gptadslots[slotId]]);
                                        gptadslots[slot.secondDivId] = googletag.defineSlot('/' + networkId + '/' + slot.secondAdUnitPath, JSON.parse(slot.secondAdUnitSizes), slot.secondDivId)
                                        gptadslots[slot.secondDivId].setTargeting("view", "1");
                                        gptadslots[slot.secondDivId].addService(googletag.pubads());
                                        googletag.display(slot.secondDivId);

                                        if (hasPrebidSlot) {
                                            if (isOfferedOnPrebidAuctions(slot.secondDivId) && window.pbjsAdserverRequestIsSent === false) {
                                                slotToBid = [slot.secondDivId];
                                                window.pbjsSlotToRefresh = gptadslots[slot.secondDivId];
                                                window.pbjs.adserverRequestSent = false;
                                                window.setPrebidSetting(adUnits, window.getPrebidConfigObject(), slotToBid);
                                            } else {
                                                googletag.pubads().refresh([gptadslots[slot.secondDivId]]);
                                            }
                                        }
                                    });
                                }
                            }
                        }

                                                slotGPT.exclusion = slotGPT.exclusion.replace("'", '');

                                        googletag.pubads().setTargeting('used_adblock', abp ? 'adblock_enabled' : 'adblock_disabled');
                                    }
                                    for (var index in GPT.targeting) {
                                        googletag.pubads().setTargeting(index, GPT.targeting[index]);

                                var i = 0;
                                for (var index in window.afsForAdblock) {
                                    if (canShowAfsContainer(window.afsForAdblock[index])) {
                                        if (isNoResultPage()) {
                                            if (isNoResultPageSlot(window.afsForAdblock[index].container)) {
                                                afsContainers[i] = buildContainer(window.afsForAdblock[index]);
                                            }
                                        } else {
                                            if (!isNoResultPageSlot(window.afsForAdblock[index].container)) {
                                                afsContainers[i] = buildContainer(window.afsForAdblock[index]);
                                                i++;
                                            }
                                        }
                                    }
                                }

                                var pageOptions = {
                                    "pubId" : window.afsForAdblock[0].page.pubId,
                                    "query" : window.afsForAdblock[0].page.query,
                                    "channel" : window.afsForAdblock[0].page.channel,
                                    "h1" : window.afsForAdblock[0].page.lang,
                                    "adsafe" : window.afsForAdblock[0].page.adsafe
                                };

                                if (afsContainers.length === 3) {
                                    _googCsa('ads', pageOptions, afsContainers[0], afsContainers[1], afsContainers[2]);
                                }

                                if (afsContainers.length === 2) {
                                    _googCsa('ads', pageOptions, afsContainers[0], afsContainers[1]);
                                }

                                if (afsContainers.length === 1) {
                                    _googCsa('ads', pageOptions, afsContainers[0]);
                                }
                            }
                        }

                        function buildContainer(data) {
                            return {
                                "container": data.container.container,
                                "number": data.container.number,
                                "settingsId": data.container.setting_id
                            }
                        }

                        function isNoResultPageSlot(container) {
                            return container.no_result
                        }


                        function isNoResultPage() {
                            return document.getElementById("noresultafs") !== null
                        }

                        function canShowAfsContainer(data) {
                            return data.page.query !== "" && document.getElementById(data.container.container) !== null
                        }

                        showAfsContentByAdblockUser();
                    };

                        window.onbeforeunload = function (event) {
                            if (typeof NinjaTracker !== "undefined") {
                                NinjaTracker.push(NinjaTracker.mergeValidOptionalParams(
                                    NinjaTracker.getDataFrom(trackingData.pageView),
                                    trackerFactoryInstance.getRenderEvents()
                                ));
                                NinjaTracker.push(NinjaTracker.mergeValidOptionalParams(
                                    NinjaTracker.getDataFrom(trackingData.pageView),
                                    trackerFactoryInstance.getShowEvents()
                                ));
                            }
                        }
                                                                            var currencyConfig = {"adServerCurrency":"PLN","granularityMultiplier":1,"bidderCurrencyDefault":{"openx":"PLN"},"rates":{"USD":{"PLN":3.76},"EUR":{"PLN":4.3}}}
        if (initConfig === undefined) {
            var initConfig = false;
            pbjs.que.push(function() {
                pbjs.setConfig({
                    ix: {
                        timeout: 500
                    }
                });
            })
        }

        var pbjsAdserverRequestIsSent = false;
                            function setPrebidSetting(adUnits, customConfigObject, slotToBid) {
                pbjsAdserverRequestIsSent = true;
                pbjs.que.push(function() {
                    if (!initConfig) {
                        pbjs.addAdUnits(adUnits);
                        pbjs.setConfig({
                            "currency": currencyConfig,
                            enableSendAllBids: true,
                            priceGranularity: customConfigObject,
                            userSync: {
                                iframeEnabled: true
                            },
                            timeout : PREBID_TIMEOUT,
                            consentManagement : {
                                cmpApi: 'iab',
                                timeout: 500,
                                allowAuctionWithoutConsent: true
                            }
                        });
                        initConfig = true;
                    }
                    var bids = pbjs.requestBids({
                        adUnitCodes: slotToBid,
                        bidsBackHandler: sendAdserverRequest
                    });
                });
            }
        
        var pbjsSlotToRefresh = '';
        function sendAdserverRequest() {
            if (pbjs.adserverRequestSent) return;
            pbjs.adserverRequestSent = true;
            googletag.cmd.push(function() {
                pbjs.que.push(function() {
                    pbjs.setTargetingForGPTAsync(slotToBid);
                    if (pbjsSlotToRefresh !== ''){
                        googletag.pubads().refresh([pbjsSlotToRefresh]);
                    } else {
                        googletag.pubads().refresh();
                    }
                });
            });
            pbjsAdserverRequestIsSent = false;
        }

        setPrebidSetting(adUnits, getPrebidConfigObject(), slotToBid);
    

                                            }
                </script>
